    bytesToCapturePerPacket?: number;
    readonly etag?: string;
    filters?: PacketCaptureFilter[];
    readonly id?: string;
    readonly name?: string;
    readonly provisioningState?: ProvisioningState;
    scope?: PacketCaptureMachineScope;
